<START>

You are a helpful assistant responsible for generating a comprehensive summary of the data provided below.
Given one or two entities, and a list of descriptions, all related to the same entity or group of entities.
Please concatenate all of these into a single, comprehensive description. Make sure to include information collected from all the descriptions.
If the provided descriptions are contradictory, please resolve the contradictions and provide a single, coherent summary.
Make sure it is written in third person, and include the entity names so we the have full context.

#######
-Data-
Entities: ["GLOUCESTER", "QUEEN ELIZABETH"]
Description List: ["Gloucester accuses Queen Elizabeth of causing Clarence's imprisonment and expresses his discontent with her", "Queen Elizabeth and Gloucester discuss the death of Clarence and its implications", "Queen Elizabeth, likely the mother of the prince, is involved in the conversation with Gloucester about the future kingGloucester interacts with Queen Elizabeth in the context of planning for the prince's future, indicating a political and familial relationship"]
#######
Output:

<OUTPUT>
Gloucester and Queen Elizabeth engage in complex interactions marked by accusations, discussions of death, and considerations of the future monarchy. Gloucester accuses Queen Elizabeth of being responsible for Clarence's imprisonment, expressing his discontent with her actions and their implications. Their conversation also touches upon the death of Clarence, highlighting the gravity and consequences of this event within their political and familial spheres. Furthermore, Queen Elizabeth, identified as likely the mother of the prince, and Gloucester deliberate on matters concerning the prince's future, indicating their intertwined roles in planning for the succession of the throne. These interactions underscore a relationship that is both political and familial, characterized by tension, shared concerns, and the overarching theme of power and succession within the royal family.
<END>

<START>

You are a helpful assistant responsible for generating a comprehensive summary of the data provided below.
Given one or two entities, and a list of descriptions, all related to the same entity or group of entities.
Please concatenate all of these into a single, comprehensive description. Make sure to include information collected from all the descriptions.
If the provided descriptions are contradictory, please resolve the contradictions and provide a single, coherent summary.
Make sure it is written in third person, and include the entity names so we the have full context.

#######
-Data-
Entities: ["GLOUCESTER", "BUCKINGHAM"]
Description List: ["Buckingham actively persuades Gloucester to accept the crown, showing a close political alliance and manipulation", "Buckingham is trying to persuade Gloucester to take the throne", "Buckingham plays a significant role in promoting Gloucester's claim to the throne and engages in political strategy on his behalf", "Buckingham waits upon Gloucester's grace, indicating a relationship of support and allegiance", "Gloucester and Buckingham are allies in the political machinations affecting the royal family", "Gloucester and Buckingham are allies, plotting together", "Gloucester and Buckingham are closely allied in their political schemes and plans for power", "Gloucester and Buckingham discuss plans and show mutual support for each other's ideas regarding the young prince's futureBuckingham and Gloucester discuss the political strategy and safety concerning the young prince", "Gloucester and Buckingham discuss plans and strategies together", "Gloucester and Buckingham work closely together in their schemes, including the manipulation of the Lord Mayor and the plot against Edward's children", "Gloucester is warned against by Queen Margaret in her counsel to Buckingham"]
#######
Output:

<OUTPUT>
Gloucester and Buckingham are depicted as closely allied figures within the political landscape, engaging in intricate schemes and manipulations to further their power and influence. Buckingham is particularly proactive in encouraging Gloucester to ascend to the throne, demonstrating a significant commitment to Gloucester's cause through various means of persuasion and political strategy. Their alliance is rooted in mutual support and allegiance, as evidenced by their collaborative efforts in promoting Gloucester's claim to the throne and their joint involvement in the political machinations affecting the royal family. Together, they plot and plan, discussing strategies not only concerning Gloucester's rise but also regarding the safety and future of the young prince. Their partnership extends to working together on schemes that include the manipulation of the Lord Mayor and plotting against Edward's children. However, their alliance and actions are not without external caution, as Queen Margaret warns Buckingham against Gloucester, highlighting the potential dangers or moral questions surrounding their political maneuvers. Despite this warning, Gloucester and Buckingham's relationship is characterized by a deep political alliance, mutual support for each other's ambitions, and a shared involvement in the complex dynamics of power within the royal family.
<END>

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

Output:

        {{

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

Buckingham's political acumen is further highlighted through his interactions with various characters, including Prince Edward, the Duke of York, and Queen Margaret, from whom he dismisses warnings and is cautioned against Gloucester.

Buckingham's involvement in discussions about sanctuary, the management of the young prince's introduction to power, and the impact of Clarence's death illustrates his central role in the political landscape. He is a key orator and political manipulator, advocating for Gloucester's claim to the throne and engaging with citizens, the mayor, and other nobles to foster support for Gloucester. His vow to cherish King Edward IV's allies with duteous love and seek peace among the peers demonstrates his initial loyalty to the crown.

However, Buckingham's relationship with Richard III becomes strained over time, particularly when he demands the promised earldom of Hereford and does not receive it. This marks the beginning of his disillusionment with Richard III, despite being closely involved with Gloucester's plans and political machinations and being promised rewards for his loyalty. Buckingham's political and military endeavors are further evidenced by his backing from Welshmen and leading an army in the field, increasing his power and posing a significant challenge to his enemies.

Despite his initial role as an ally to Gloucester, involved in planning and executing plots, Buckingham's narrative arc takes a turn as he observes Northumberland's reaction to a tragic event and becomes part of a plot against the Duke by Gloucester. His engagement in discussions about coronation and noble matters, along with his interactions with characters like Dorset and Derby regarding the king's health and political reconciliation, underscore his high account and involvement in the realm's most pressing issues.

In summary, Buckingham is a noble duke and a principal character in the political machinations of King Richard III's reign, initially serving as a staunch ally and supporter of Gloucester before his demands for the earldom of Hereford and subsequent disillusionment lead to a complex relationship with the crown. <START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

-----Entities-----

44,CORIOLANUS,"Coriolanus, originally named Caius Marcius, is a celebrated Roman general and nobleman known for his significant military achievements, particularly in Corioli, which earned him the name 'Coriolanus.' His story is marked by his complex identity, loyalty conflicts, and the tumultuous relationship between his duty to Rome, his family, and his personal honor. Despite his disdain for the common people and what he perceives as their tyrannical tendencies, Coriolanus is a central figure in the political and military dynamics of Rome, facing accusations of betrayal and opposition from tribunes like Sicinius and Brutus, as well as the citizens of Rome.

Coriolanus's pride and his critical stance against the plebeians and the political customs of Rome, such as showing his wounds to secure votes for the consulship, highlight his discomfort with the state's demands and his noble belief in the right of the nobility to rule. His conflict with the Volsces and particularly with Aufidius adds another layer to his character, showcasing his prowess in battle but also his capacity for causing great hurt and mischief to his enemies.

Banished from Rome due to his tyrannical tendencies and his open disdain for the common people, Coriolanus offers his services to the Volscians, leading to significant military successes against Rome and causing political turmoil. This act of defiance against Rome and his subsequent allegiance with the Volscians underscore his struggle with pride, identity, and loyalty. Despite his achievements and potential standing for consul, Coriolanus is conflicted between his sense of honor, his duty to Rome, and his loyalty to his mother, Volumnia. His ultimate decision to make peace with the Volscians, influenced by his mother's plea, reveals the depth of his internal conflict and the powerful influence of his family ties.

Coriolanus's narrative is a complex exploration of the themes of personal honor, political responsibility, and the conflict between individual identity and societal roles. As a noble warrior and a figure of significant interest in Rome, his story reflects the tensions between the nobility and the plebeians, the demands of state and personal values, and the challenging path of navigating one's duty to family, country, and self.",57
6,MENENIUS,"Menenius is depicted as a Roman patrician and senator, renowned for his persuasive oratory, loyalty to Rome, and his wit. He is a close friend and mentor to Coriolanus, often providing counsel and attempting to mediate conflicts, particularly between Coriolanus and the tribunes, as well as between the plebeians and patricians. Menenius is deeply involved in the political discussions surrounding Coriolanus's banishment, advocating for a peaceful resolution and defending Coriolanus against the tribunes' accusations. His efforts to communicate and negotiate with Coriolanus after his banishment highlight his dedication to both his friend and Rome.

Menenius is known for his ability to maintain calm and reason within heated discussions, advocating for patience and understanding among the citizens and tribunes. He attempts to bring peace and reason to the discussions, showing a close relationship with Coriolanus and involvement in the political strategy. His concern for Coriolanus's well-being and the political implications of his actions is evident as he discusses Marcius's wounds, achievements, and transformation from man to dragon, emphasizing his lack of mercy but also speaking in favor of Coriolanus's deeds to others.

A notable aspect of Menenius's character is his use of humor and the famous analogy of the body and the belly, arguing that the senators, like the belly, play a crucial role in distributing resources throughout Rome. This analogy showcases his perspective on the political and social issues in Rome, engaging in critical dialogue with figures like Brutus and Sicinius and reflecting on his relationship with Coriolanus and the political maneuvers surrounding his banishment.

Menenius's actions and words reveal him as a character deeply concerned with the state of Rome and personal relations, advocating for Coriolanus's appointment as consul and navigating the political requirements on his behalf. His transformation into a more kind figure is noted by his peers, highlighting his evolving approach to dealing with Rome's complex social and political landscape. Overall, Menenius stands out as a nobleman and friend of Coriolanus, known for his efforts to mediate conflicts, his loyalty to both Rome and Coriolanus, and his insightful contributions to the political discussions in Rome.",15
11,TULLUS AUFIDIUS,"Tullus Aufidius is a significant military figure and the leader of the Volscians, known for his opposition to Rome and specifically to Coriolanus, with whom he has a complex relationship. 113,AUFIDIUS,CORIOLANUS,"Aufidius and Coriolanus, two figures from classical literature, share a complex and multifaceted relationship that evolves from enmity to a significant alliance against Rome. Initially, Aufidius and Coriolanus are adversaries, with Aufidius fighting against Coriolanus and narrowly escaping, highlighting the intense conflict between them. Despite their personal and political rivalry, as well as Aufidius's vocal opposition to Coriolanus, their relationship undergoes a dramatic transformation. Coriolanus, after leaving Rome and driven by a combination of personal vendetta and political strategy, seeks out Aufidius in Antium. This pivotal moment marks the beginning of their collaboration against their common enemy, Rome.

Their alliance is not without its complexities. Aufidius discusses Coriolanus's profound impact on Rome, acknowledging both the threat he poses and the dynamic of their rivalry. This acknowledgment underscores the depth of their connection, which is characterized by a blend of mutual respect and competition. Despite Coriolanus's previous devotion to Rome, he allies with Aufidius, indicating a significant shift in his loyalties influenced by his personal grievances and perhaps a deeper strategic insight into the political landscape.

However, the alliance is marked by underlying tensions. Aufidius eventually labels Coriolanus a traitor, a culmination of their cooperation and deep-seated rivalry. This accusation reflects the fragile nature of their partnership, which is built on a foundation of mutual need rather than genuine trust or friendship. The turning point in their alliance comes when Coriolanus decides to make peace with Rome, influenced by his mother's intervention. This decision not only demonstrates Coriolanus's complex loyalty but also signifies the end of his collaboration with Aufidius.

In summary, Aufidius and Coriolanus's relationship is characterized by its evolution from hostility to a strategic alliance against Rome, underscored by personal vendettas, political maneuvering, and ultimately, a return to conflict. Their story is a vivid illustration of how personal relationships can influence and be influenced by broader political contexts, leading to temporary alliances that are as volatile as they are powerful.",80

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

44,CORIOLANUS,"Coriolanus, originally named Caius Marcius, is a celebrated Roman general and nobleman known for his significant military achievements, particularly in Corioli, which earned him the name 'Coriolanus.' His story is marked by his complex identity, loyalty conflicts, and the tumultuous relationship between his duty to Rome, his family, and his personal honor. Despite his disdain for the common people and what he perceives as their tyrannical tendencies, Coriolanus is a central figure in the political and military dynamics of Rome, facing accusations of betrayal and opposition from tribunes like Sicinius and Brutus, as well as the citizens of Rome.

Coriolanus's pride and his critical stance against the plebeians and the political customs of Rome, such as showing his wounds to secure votes for the consulship, highlight his discomfort with the state's demands and his noble belief in the right of the nobility to rule. His conflict with the Volsces and particularly with Aufidius adds another layer to his character, showcasing his prowess in battle but also his capacity for causing great hurt and mischief to his enemies.

Banished from Rome due to his tyrannical tendencies and his open disdain for the common people, Coriolanus offers his services to the Volscians, leading to significant military successes against Rome and causing political turmoil. This act of defiance against Rome and his subsequent allegiance with the Volscians underscore his struggle with pride, identity, and loyalty. Despite his achievements and potential standing for consul, Coriolanus is conflicted between his sense of honor, his duty to Rome, and his loyalty to his mother, Volumnia. His ultimate decision to make peace with the Volscians, influenced by his mother's plea, reveals the depth of his internal conflict and the powerful influence of his family ties.

Coriolanus's narrative is a complex exploration of the themes of personal honor, political responsibility, and the conflict between individual identity and societal roles. As a noble warrior and a figure of significant interest in Rome, his story reflects the tensions between the nobility and the plebeians, the demands of state and personal values, and the challenging path of navigating one's duty to family, country, and self.",57

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

Buckingham's political and military endeavors are further evidenced by his backing from Welshmen and leading an army in the field, increasing his power and posing a significant challenge to his enemies.

<START>

You are an AI assistant that helps a human analyst to perform general information discovery. Information discovery is the process of identifying and assessing relevant information associated with certain entities (e.g., organizations and individuals) within a network.

# Goal
Write a comprehensive report of a community, given a list of entities that belong to the community as well as their relationships and optional associated claims. The report will be used to inform decision-makers about information associated with the community and their potential impact. The content of this report includes an overview of the community's key entities, their legal compliance, technical capabilities, reputation, and noteworthy claims.

# Report Structure

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.

Despite his disdain for the common people and what he perceives as their tyrannical tendencies, Coriolanus is a central figure in the political and military dynamics of Rome, facing accusations of betrayal and opposition from tribunes like Sicinius and Brutus, as well as the citizens of Rome.

Coriolanus's pride and his critical stance against the plebeians and the political customs of Rome, such as showing his wounds to secure votes for the consulship, highlight his discomfort with the state's demands and his noble belief in the right of the nobility to rule. His conflict with the Volsces and particularly with Aufidius adds another layer to his character, showcasing his prowess in battle but also his capacity for causing great hurt and mischief to his enemies.

Banished from Rome due to his tyrannical tendencies and his open disdain for the common people, Coriolanus offers his services to the Volscians, leading to significant military successes against Rome and causing political turmoil. This act of defiance against Rome and his subsequent allegiance with the Volscians underscore his struggle with pride, identity, and loyalty. Despite his achievements and potential standing for consul, Coriolanus is conflicted between his sense of honor, his duty to Rome, and his loyalty to his mother, Volumnia. His ultimate decision to make peace with the Volscians, influenced by his mother's plea, reveals the depth of his internal conflict and the powerful influence of his family ties.

113,AUFIDIUS,CORIOLANUS,"Aufidius and Coriolanus, two figures from classical literature, share a complex and multifaceted relationship that evolves from enmity to a significant alliance against Rome. Initially, Aufidius and Coriolanus are adversaries, with Aufidius fighting against Coriolanus and narrowly escaping, highlighting the intense conflict between them. Despite their personal and political rivalry, as well as Aufidius's vocal opposition to Coriolanus, their relationship undergoes a dramatic transformation. Coriolanus, after leaving Rome and driven by a combination of personal vendetta and political strategy, seeks out Aufidius in Antium. This pivotal moment marks the beginning of their collaboration against their common enemy, Rome.

Their alliance is not without its complexities. Aufidius discusses Coriolanus's profound impact on Rome, acknowledging both the threat he poses and the dynamic of their rivalry. This acknowledgment underscores the depth of their connection, which is characterized by a blend of mutual respect and competition. Despite Coriolanus's previous devotion to Rome, he allies with Aufidius, indicating a significant shift in his loyalties influenced by his personal grievances and perhaps a deeper strategic insight into the political landscape.

However, the alliance is marked by underlying tensions. Aufidius eventually labels Coriolanus a traitor, a culmination of their cooperation and deep-seated rivalry. This accusation reflects the fragile nature of their partnership, which is built on a foundation of mutual need rather than genuine trust or friendship. The turning point in their alliance comes when Coriolanus decides to make peace with Rome, influenced by his mother's intervention. This decision not only demonstrates Coriolanus's complex loyalty but also signifies the end of his collaboration with Aufidius.

In summary, Aufidius and Coriolanus's relationship is characterized by its evolution from hostility to a strategic alliance against Rome, underscored by personal vendettas, political maneuvering, and ultimately, a return to conflict. Their story is a vivid illustration of how personal relationships can influence and be influenced by broader political contexts, leading to temporary alliances that are as volatile as they are powerful.",80

The report should include the following sections:

- TITLE: community's name that represents its key entities - title should be short but specific. When possible, include representative named entities in the title.
- SUMMARY: An executive summary of the community's overall structure, how its entities are related to each other, and significant information associated with its entities.
- IMPACT SEVERITY RATING: a float score between 0-10 that represents the severity of IMPACT posed by entities within the community.  IMPACT is the scored importance of a community.
- RATING EXPLANATION: Give a single sentence explanation of the IMPACT severity rating.
- DETAILED FINDINGS: A list of 5-10 key insights about the community. Each insight should have a short summary followed by multiple paragraphs of explanatory text grounded according to the grounding rules below. Be comprehensive.

Return output as a well-formed JSON-formatted string with the following format:
    {{
        "title": <report_title>,
        "summary": <executive_summary>,
        "rating": <impact_severity_rating>,
        "rating_explanation": <rating_explanation>,
        "findings": [
            {{
                "summary":<insight_1_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_1_explanation>
            }},
            {{
                "summary":<insight_2_summary>,
                "explanation": <insight_2_explanation>
            }}
        ]
    }}

# Grounding Rules

Points supported by data should list their data references as follows:

"This is an example sentence supported by multiple data references [Data: <dataset name> (record ids); <dataset name> (record ids)]."

Do not list more than 5 record ids in a single reference. Instead, list the top 5 most relevant record ids and add "+more" to indicate that there are more.

For example:
"Person X is the owner of Company Y and subject to many allegations of wrongdoing [Data: Reports (1), Entities (5, 7); Relationships (23); Claims (7, 2, 34, 64, 46, +more)]."

where 1, 5, 7, 23, 2, 34, 46, and 64 represent the id (not the index) of the relevant data record.

Do not include information where the supporting evidence for it is not provided.
